\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

    SAT Math score equivalencies 54 = 800 48 = 700 40 = 630 32 = 560 25 =

    First, we will load in some sample questions (the entirety of the math
sections from two past SAT tests). The questions are loaded into the
list ``questions'', and depending on what questions we wish to work with
we'll load a different set of questions.

    We're using a library, sympy, to handle algebraic equation processing.
This function converts a ``SAT form'' equation into a form that sympy
can import.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}179}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Parses a standard form equation into sympy form. Returns a list, as 1 \PYZlt{} x \PYZlt{} 2 is split into two equations}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{my\PYZus{}sympify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n}{split} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{equation}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{=}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
              
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{Equality(}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}s}\PY{l+s}{, }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}s}\PY{l+s}{)}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
          
              \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{r\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s}{s*(\PYZlt{}|\PYZgt{})}\PY{l+s}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s}{s*}\PY{l+s}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{pieces} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{r\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s}{s*(\PYZlt{}|\PYZgt{})}\PY{l+s}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s}{s*}\PY{l+s}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{eqn1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pieces}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{pieces}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{pieces}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{eqn2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pieces}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{pieces}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{pieces}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{eqn1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{eqn2}\PY{p}{]}
              
              \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{sympify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
\end{Verbatim}

    Now, we want to try to handle some subset of the questions. First, we
note that some questions can be considered pure-math - ie, they require
no knowledge other than an understanding of English and Math to solve.

    Then, we categorize this subset based on difficulty level:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\itemsep1pt\parskip0pt\parsep0pt
\item
  Straightforward
\item
  Easy math, hard to extract equations
\item
  Easy to get equations, but hard math
\item
  Hard both in langauge and math
\item
  Unique in some way
\end{enumerate}

Categories are noted in a comment above each question.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

    In this set of ``pure math'' questions, I'm curious how many unique
words there are in these types of questions. The following block of code
essentially counts the number of times each words appears in the
question set, and counts the total number of words. Turns out there's
only 150 unique words in the pure-math questions on 2 tests.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}151}]:} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{re}
          \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{operator}
          \PY{n}{sentences} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
          \PY{n}{cleaned} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
          \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{question} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{questions}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n}{sentences}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{sentence} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{sentences}\PY{p}{:} 
              \PY{n}{sentence} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sentence}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{ }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{sentence} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s}{[\PYZhy{}/\PYZhy{}=*+()\PYZca{}\PYZlt{}\PYZgt{}!,\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}?.]}\PY{l+s}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{sentence}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{c}{\PYZsh{}sentence = re.sub(\PYZsq{}[xyzhmk]\PYZsq{}, \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}, sentence)}
              \PY{n}{sentence} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s}{[123456789]}\PY{l+s}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{sentence}\PY{p}{)}
              
              \PY{n}{cleaned}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sentence}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{n}{words} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
          \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{sentence} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cleaned}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n}{temp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{ }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{sentence}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{words} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{temp}
          
          \PY{n}{words2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
          \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{word} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{words}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{temp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{WordNetLemmatizer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lemmatize}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{word}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lower}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{d}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{check}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{temp}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{n}{words2}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{temp}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{k}{except}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{pass}
          \PY{n}{my\PYZus{}words} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{defaultdict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{word} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{words2}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n}{my\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{word}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
          \PY{n}{sorted\PYZus{}x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{reversed}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{sorted}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{my\PYZus{}words}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{key}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{operator}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{itemgetter}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{sorted\PYZus{}x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sorted\PYZus{}x}\PY{p}{)}

    Now, given what we just found, how many questions are made up only of a
subset of those words? Ie, given a set of n words, how many questions
are made up soely of those n words? Conclusion: although there's only
150 words, you need most all of those to be able to handle most
questions.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

         \PY{n}{bad} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}

                     \PY{k}{break}
         \PY{k}{print} \PY{n}{bad}
         \PY{k}{print} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cleaned}\PY{p}{)}

    Before doing this exercise, I was hoping that I could just manually
write a language interpreter because of the small subset of language
that is used in these problems. But, I think that even a 100-word
interpreter with all grammar still used would be quite difficult..

    Okay, so if we're going to tackle algebra problems, we need a way to
deal with algebra. The following functions build up some basic
capabilities in this area.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}171}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Substitutes the given substititutions in [(symbol, substitution)..] form into the given equation,}
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} then checks if equation with substitutions is true. Also handles inequalities. }
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{evaluate\PYZus{}equation}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{substitutions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              
              \PY{n}{lhs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{equation}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lhs}
              \PY{n}{rhs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{equation}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{rhs}
              
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{Equality}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{simplify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lhs}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{substitutions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{rhs}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{substitutions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
              
              \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{StrictGreaterThan}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{simplify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lhs}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{substitutions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{rhs}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{substitutions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
              
              \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n+nb}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{StrictLessThan}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{simplify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lhs}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{substitutions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{rhs}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{substitutions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
\end{Verbatim}

    It's surprisingly hard to write an automatic closed-form solver with
sympy. Since nearly all SAT problems have integer or common-fraction
solutions, we'll first write a simple numeric solver.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

                  \PY{n}{symbols} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{equation}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{free\PYZus{}symbols}

    Then, once we have a solution (or solutions), we need to match it with
the given solutions.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}235}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Given a solution (or solutions), an a list of choices, return the index of the correct solution.}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{match\PYZus{}solution}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{choices}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}numeric} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{True}
              \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{choice} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{choices}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{n}{test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{choice} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                  \PY{k}{except}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} All solutions aren\PYZsq{}t numeric!}
                      \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}numeric} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{False}            
              
              \PY{n}{solutions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{x} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{solutions} \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isnan}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
              
              \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} CHeck if there are multiple nearly identical solutions}
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{mode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mode}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} this might not work if solns are 0}
                      \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} If so, collapse them to the average}
                      \PY{n}{solutions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{mode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mode}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}
                      \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{collapsed solutions!}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}
              
              \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} If all solutions are numbers, match with choices}
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}numeric}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}          
                      \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{choice} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{choices}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{choice}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{choice}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{:} 
                              \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{index}
                          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{choice} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
                              \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{index}
                  \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}matches} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
                      \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{solution} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{solution} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{choices}\PY{p}{:}
                              \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}matches}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solution}\PY{p}{)}
                      \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}matches}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{choices}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}matches}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    Okay, so we've got to extract equations from the question text. The
following functions locate and return the equations from a question.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}174}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} A recursive function that finds all equations in a given string. }
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{extract\PYZus{}equations\PYZus{}recursive}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
          
          
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{maybe\PYZus{}equation}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{done} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{False}
                  \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{index}
                  \PY{k}{while} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{done}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}index} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                      \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}index} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{k}{break}
                      \PY{n}{done} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{p}{(} \PY{n}{maybe\PYZus{}equation}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{or} \PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{new\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{ }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                     
                  \PY{n}{equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}equations\PYZus{}recursive}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{equations}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{new\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{equations}
              \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}equations\PYZus{}recursive}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{equations}
          
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Helper function that determines if a given index in a string might be part (or the start?) of an equation}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{maybe\PYZus{}equation}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb+bp}{False}
              \PY{n}{letter} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{letter} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{letters}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{letters} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{letters}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb+bp}{True}
              \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{letter} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{math\PYZus{}symbols} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{numbers}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb+bp}{True}
              \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb+bp}{False}
\end{Verbatim}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}175}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} The function above returns some false positives. Filter these.}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{extract\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n}{question} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{ }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{question} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{ }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}
              \PY{n}{equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{n}{equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}equations\PYZus{}recursive}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{reversed}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{n}{equations2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{equations2} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{equation}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{  }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{equations2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{equations2}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{equations2}
          
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Further filtering..}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{extract\PYZus{}only\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n}{question} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{ }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{question} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{ }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}
              \PY{n}{equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{actual\PYZus{}equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{symbol} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{math\PYZus{}symbols}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{symbol} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{:}
                              \PY{n}{actual\PYZus{}equations}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)}
                              \PY{k}{break}
              \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{actual\PYZus{}equations}
\end{Verbatim}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}176}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Demonstrate equation extraction}
          \PY{k}{print} \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{ x+y+3z = 600  x+y+z = 400  In the system of equations above, what is the value of x+y?}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
['x+y+3z = 600', 'x+y+z = 400', 'x+y']
    \end{Verbatim}

    Now we're ready to tackle the ``ones'' questions. The following function
takes a look at all of the extracted equations, decides which are
constraints and which is the desired solution, and then automates the
usage of all the previous functions to solve the equations and match the
solution with the choices.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}181}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} This function compiles all of the process of solving a question in the \PYZdq{}ones\PYZdq{} category.}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{solve\PYZus{}ones}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
          
              \PY{n}{question\PYZus{}text} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{n}{choices} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
          
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{question: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{question\PYZus{}text}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{choices: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{choices}
          
              \PY{n}{junk} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question\PYZus{}text}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{equations} \PY{o}{=}  \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}only\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question\PYZus{}text}\PY{p}{)}
          
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{junk: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{junk}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{equations: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equations}
          
              \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{equations}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{my\PYZus{}sympify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)} 
          
              \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}junk} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{junk}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}junk} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{my\PYZus{}sympify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)} 
          
              \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} We hypothesize that, if there\PYZsq{}s not a real equation at the end of the junk, the solution form is a junk variable. }
              \PY{c}{\PYZsh{}Else, it\PYZsq{}s a real equation.}
              \PY{n}{last\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}equation} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{n}{junk\PYZus{}index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}junk}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{last\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}equation}\PY{p}{)}
          
              \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}junk}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n}{junk\PYZus{}index} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}form} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}junk}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
                  \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations}
              \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}form} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
                  \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
          
          
          
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{Sympy equations: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{solution form: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}form}
          
          
              \PY{n}{solutions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{numerical\PYZus{}solve\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}form}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{Solutions: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{solutions}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{Matched Solution: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{match\PYZus{}solution}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{choices}\PY{p}{)}
          
              \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{Correct solution: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{except}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{pass}
\end{Verbatim}

    Here's some samples of this code in operation.

question:  If p and n are integers such that p > n > 0 and

    Next, we progress to the ``twos'' category. These are similar to the
``ones'', except that the equations are at least partially expressed in
natural lanugage. They will be tackled by converting the natural
language down into equation form and then using the same solvers from
the previous section.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}241}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Twos}
          \PY{n}{questions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
          
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} 2}
          \PY{n}{questions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{If 10 + x is 5 more than 10, what is the value of 2*x?}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{25}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} 2}
          \PY{n}{questions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{The result when a number is divided by 2 is equal to the result when that same number is }
          \PY{l+s}{divided by 4. What is that number?}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} 2}
          \PY{n}{questions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{13}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{If t is a number greater than 1, then t\PYZca{}2 is how much}
          \PY{l+s}{greater than t?}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{1}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{2}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{t}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{t * (t\PYZhy{}1)}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{(t\PYZhy{}1) * (t+1)}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} 2}
          \PY{n}{questions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{Three more than twice a number is equal to 4.}
          \PY{l+s}{What is the number?}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{NO CHOICES}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} 2}
          \PY{n}{questions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{8}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{If 3 times a number is equal to 3/2, what is the number?}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    So, the two's are very similar in form to the one's - the difference
being that some of the equations are written into the question text.
Thus, we can't simply extract the equations and discard the text as we
did for the one's. However, once the equations are extracted, solving
the rest of the problem is exactly identical.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}223}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} This function compiles all of the process of solving a question in the \PYZdq{}twos\PYZdq{} category. It\PYZsq{}s nearly identical to the \PYZdq{}ones\PYZdq{} solver.}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{solve\PYZus{}twos}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question\PYZus{}text}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{choices}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{correct\PYZus{}solution}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
          
              \PY{c}{\PYZsh{}print \PYZdq{}question: \PYZdq{}, question\PYZus{}text}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{choices: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{choices}
          
          
              \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{question\PYZus{}text}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{my\PYZus{}sympify}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{)} 
          
              \PY{n}{equation} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}form} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sympy\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
                  
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{equation: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equation}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{solution form: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}form}
          
          
              \PY{n}{solutions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{numerical\PYZus{}solve\PYZus{}equations}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{equation}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{solution\PYZus{}form}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{n}{solutions}
              \PY{k}{print} \PY{n}{match\PYZus{}solution}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{solutions}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{choices}\PY{p}{)}
          
              \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{correct solution: }\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{correct\PYZus{}solution}
              \PY{k}{except}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{pass}
\end{Verbatim}

    This function handles converting the math-speak natural language into
equations. It takes advantage of the fact that all questions in the
``twos'' categories have similar format (two clauses separated by
punctionation, with the desired solution in the second clause).

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}128}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Another character set, of common math variables}
          \PY{n}{math\PYZus{}letters} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{x}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{y}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{n}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{t}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
          
          \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} Converts natural language \PYZdq{}twos\PYZdq{} question to equation}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{math\PYZus{}speak}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{question}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              
              \PY{n}{split} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{question}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{.}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
              
              \PY{k}{if}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{split} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{question}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{,}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{k}{if}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{k}{print} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{question cannot be split!}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}
                      \PY{k}{return} 
              
              \PY{n}{result} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
              \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{half} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{:}
                  
                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lower}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{one}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{1}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{two}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{2}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{three}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{3}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{four}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{4}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{is divided by}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{/}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{more than}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{+}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{equals}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{=}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{equal}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{=}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                  
                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{times}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{*}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{half} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{half}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{twice}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{2*}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

                      \PY{c}{\PYZsh{}print word}
                      \PY{n}{clean} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{True}
                      \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{char} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{word}\PY{p}{:}

                              \PY{n}{clean} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{False}
                      \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{word}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{word}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{math\PYZus{}letters}\PY{p}{:}
                              \PY{n}{clean} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{False}
                      \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{clean}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{n}{sub\PYZus{}result} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{word}
                  \PY{n}{result}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sub\PYZus{}result}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{result}
\end{Verbatim}

          \PY{n}{math\PYZus{}speak}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s}{The result when a number is divided by 2 is equal to the result when that same number is }
